

.. Race and Ethnicity:

Race and Ethnicity
====================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Population breakdowns by race and ethnicity. 

.. contents::
   :local:
   :depth: 10





.. _au.data.B01_Indigenous_psns_Aboriginal_F:

Indigenous Persons Aboriginal (Females)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Selected Person Characteristics





Measure "Indigenous Persons Aboriginal (Females)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B01_Indigenous_psns_Aboriginal_F'
      );





Measure "Indigenous Persons Aboriginal (Females)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
          'au.data.B01_Indigenous_psns_Aboriginal_F'
        );






Measure "Indigenous Persons Aboriginal (Females)" percent of "Total (Females)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B01_Indigenous_psns_Aboriginal_F',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Indigenous Persons Aboriginal (Females)" percent of "Total (Females)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
        'au.data.B01_Indigenous_psns_Aboriginal_F',
        'denominator'
      );

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^





Ancestry





Measure "Maltese Total Responses"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B08A_Maltese_Tot_Resp'
      );





Measure "Maltese Total Responses" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
          'au.data.B08A_Maltese_Tot_Resp'
        );






Measure "Maltese Total Responses" percent of "Total Persons Total Responses" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B08A_Maltese_Tot_Resp',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Maltese Total Responses" percent of "Total Persons Total Responses" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
        'au.data.B08A_Maltese_Tot_Resp',
        'denominator'
      );
